# Exercise 2 – Create a new plan in Planner
<p class="block_">To help organise our IT team we will assign tasks to them using Planner. A plan, in Planner is a place to assign tasks to colleagues. The colleagues you may assign tasks to are derived from the Microsoft 365 group that the plan is associated with. In this exercise we will add a plan to our existing Microsoft 365 group for IT support which came with our SharePoint site.</p>
<ol class="list_">
<li class="block_15">In the <b class="calibre6">app launcher</b> <img alt="Image" class="calibre15" src="https://raw.githubusercontent.com/WebucatorTraining/skillable/main/55283/epub/images/image-3.jpeg"/> click on <b class="calibre6">All apps</b> then choose <b class="calibre6">Planner</b><br class="calibre2"/><br class="calibre2"/><img alt="Image" class="calibre103" src="https://raw.githubusercontent.com/WebucatorTraining/skillable/main/55283/epub/images/image-39.png"/></li>
<li class="block_16">Review the <i class="calibre7">Welcome to Planner</i> pop-up then choose <b class="calibre6">Create a plan!</b><br class="calibre2"/> </li>
<li class="block_16">In the <i class="calibre7">Plan name</i> enter <b class="calibre6">Hardware Refresh</b><br class="calibre2"/> </li>
<li class="block_16">Under the title, click on <b class="calibre6">Add to an existing Microsoft 365 Group</b><br class="calibre2"/> </li>
<li class="block_16">Select the name of your Microsoft 365 Group e.g. <b class="calibre6">Chris – IT Support<br class="calibre2"/> </b></li>
<li class="block_16">Then click on <b class="calibre6">Create plan</b><br class="calibre2"/><br class="calibre2"/><img alt="Image" class="calibre104" src="https://raw.githubusercontent.com/WebucatorTraining/skillable/main/55283/epub/images/image113.png"/><br class="calibre2"/> </li>
<li class="block_16">At the top of the plan are buckets, one named <i class="calibre7">To do</i> and a button to the right offers an option to <i class="calibre7">Add new bucket</i>, click on <b class="calibre6">To do</b> and change the name of this bucket to <b class="calibre6">Laptops</b> and press <b class="calibre6">Enter</b><br class="calibre2"/><br class="calibre2"/><img alt="Image" class="calibre105" src="https://raw.githubusercontent.com/WebucatorTraining/skillable/main/55283/epub/images/image114.png"/><br class="calibre2"/> </li>
<li class="block_16">To the right of this bucket, click on <b class="calibre6">Add new bucket</b> and name the bucket <b class="calibre6">Desktops</b><br class="calibre2"/> </li>
<li class="block_16">Add a third bucket called <b class="calibre6">Phones and Tablets</b> (this may scroll the page to the right on a smaller screen, if so, scroll the browser left to view all three buckets)<br class="calibre2"/> </li>
<li class="block_16">Under the <i class="calibre7">Laptops</i> bucket choose <b class="calibre6">Add task</b><br class="calibre2"/> </li>
<li class="block_16">Enter the following data (you can enter any date you prefer)<br class="calibre2"/><br class="calibre2"/><img alt="Image" class="calibre106" src="https://raw.githubusercontent.com/WebucatorTraining/skillable/main/55283/epub/images/image115.png"/></li>
<li class="block_16">Click <b class="calibre6">Add task</b><br class="calibre2"/> </li>
<li class="block_16">Within the <i class="calibre7">Laptops</i> bucket, click on <b class="calibre6">Add task</b><br class="calibre2"/> </li>
<li class="block_16">Create another task with the following data (you can enter any date you prefer)<br class="calibre2"/><br class="calibre2"/><img alt="Image" class="calibre107" src="https://raw.githubusercontent.com/WebucatorTraining/skillable/main/55283/epub/images/image116.png"/></li>
<li class="block_16">Click on <b class="calibre6">Add task</b><br class="calibre2"/> </li>
<li class="block_16">In the <i class="calibre7">Phones and Tablets </i>bucket create two more tasks:</li>
</ol>
<ol class="list_3">
<li class="block_28">Test iPhone new model – assigned to Caroline Lee</li>
<li class="block_42">Test Samsung galaxy new model – assigned to Caroline Lee</li>
</ol>
<p class="block_43"><img alt="Image" class="calibre108" src="https://raw.githubusercontent.com/WebucatorTraining/skillable/main/55283/epub/images/image117.png"/></p>
<ol class="list_">
<li class="block_15" value="17">Click on the task named <b class="calibre6">Test iPhone new model</b><br class="calibre2"/> </li>
<li class="block_16">Next choose <b class="calibre6">Add label</b><br class="calibre2"/><br class="calibre2"/><img alt="Image" class="calibre109" src="https://raw.githubusercontent.com/WebucatorTraining/skillable/main/55283/epub/images/image-40.png"/><br class="calibre2"/> </li>
<li class="block_16">To help distinguish tasks that relate to phones and tasks that relate to tablets, we will use some labels, click on the <b class="calibre6">Edit label name</b> <img alt="Pencil" class="calibre85" src="https://raw.githubusercontent.com/WebucatorTraining/skillable/main/55283/epub/images/image-41.png"/> button next to a colour you like<br class="calibre2"/> </li>
<li class="block_16">Change the name of the label by deleting the current entry and replacing it with <b class="calibre6">Phone </b>then press <b class="calibre6">Enter</b><br class="calibre2"/> </li>
<li class="block_16">Repeat the previous two steps on a different colour, and change the current label name to <b class="calibre6">Tablet</b><br class="calibre2"/> </li>
<li class="block_16">From your labels, select <b class="calibre6">Phone</b> <br class="calibre2"/><br class="calibre2"/><img alt="Image" class="calibre110" src="https://raw.githubusercontent.com/WebucatorTraining/skillable/main/55283/epub/images/image121.png"/><br class="calibre2"/> </li>
<li class="block_16">In the tasks progress change the value <i class="calibre7">Not started</i> to <b class="calibre6">In progress</b><br class="calibre2"/> </li>
<li class="block_16">Change the priority from <i class="calibre7">Medium</i> to <b class="calibre6">Low<br class="calibre2"/> </b></li>
<li class="block_16">Scroll down to the comments section and add “<i class="calibre7">Test iPhones have arrived in IT for the workgroup, please collect when possible”</i> and click <b class="calibre6">Send</b>, Caroline will be sent an email with the comments and a link to the task each time someone adds comments to one of her tasks<br class="calibre2"/> </li>
<li class="block_16">Click away from the task form to close it<br class="calibre2"/><br class="calibre2"/><img alt="Image" class="calibre111" src="https://raw.githubusercontent.com/WebucatorTraining/skillable/main/55283/epub/images/image122.png"/><br class="calibre2"/> </li>
<li class="block_16">Click on the task named <b class="calibre6">Test Samsung galaxy new version</b> and use the <b class="calibre6">Add label </b>button to add the <b class="calibre6">Phone</b> label to this task, once done, click away from the task to close it<br class="calibre2"/> </li>
<li class="block_16">Choose <b class="calibre6">Add task</b> under the <i class="calibre7">Phones and Tablets</i> bucket and create the following task<br class="calibre2"/><br class="calibre2"/><img alt="Image" class="calibre112" src="https://raw.githubusercontent.com/WebucatorTraining/skillable/main/55283/epub/images/image-42.png"/><br class="calibre2"/> </li>
<li class="block_16">Click <b class="calibre6">Add task</b><br class="calibre2"/> </li>
<li class="block_16">Click on the task named <b class="calibre6">Test iPad mini</b> and use the <b class="calibre6">Add label </b>button to add the <b class="calibre6">Tablet</b> label to this task, once done, click away from the task to close it<br class="calibre2"/> </li>
<li class="block_16">You have hard that Ravinder has completed his work on the <i class="calibre7">Dell XPS 15</i> laptop, to compete this task, click on the <b class="calibre6">Circle</b> at the top right of the task card<br class="calibre2"/><br class="calibre2"/><img alt="Image" class="calibre113" src="https://raw.githubusercontent.com/WebucatorTraining/skillable/main/55283/epub/images/image124.png"/></li>
<li class="block_16">Click on Simon’s task named <b class="calibre6">Test Lenovo Thinkpad new version</b><br class="calibre2"/> </li>
<li class="block_16">In the <i class="calibre7">Checklist</i> section click on <b class="calibre6">Add an item</b><br class="calibre2"/> </li>
<li class="block_16">Enter <b class="calibre6">Use latest gold build for first test </b>then press <b class="calibre6">Enter</b><br class="calibre2"/> </li>
<li class="block_16">Click on the <b class="calibre6">Add an item</b> option below your previous entry and enter <b class="calibre6">Reset laptop build and try new beta build</b><br class="calibre2"/> </li>
<li class="block_16">Add another check list item for <b class="calibre6">Update review documentation with findings</b><br class="calibre2"/> </li>
<li class="block_16">Ensure that <b class="calibre6">Show on card </b>has been selected<br class="calibre2"/><br class="calibre2"/><img alt="Image" class="calibre114" src="https://raw.githubusercontent.com/WebucatorTraining/skillable/main/55283/epub/images/image125.png"/><br class="calibre2"/> </li>
<li class="block_16">Click away from the task form to close it, you should be able to see the checklist on the card, click on <b class="calibre6">Use the latest gold build for first test</b> to mark it off, it will disappear from the checklist on the card but it will still be visible when the task has been opened with a tick next to it (you can open the task to see this)<br class="calibre2"/><br class="calibre2"/><img alt="Image" class="calibre115" src="https://raw.githubusercontent.com/WebucatorTraining/skillable/main/55283/epub/images/image126.png"/></li>
<li class="block_16">At the top of the page, select <b class="calibre6">Charts</b><br class="calibre2"/><br class="calibre2"/><img alt="Image" class="calibre116" src="https://raw.githubusercontent.com/WebucatorTraining/skillable/main/55283/epub/images/image127.png"/></li>
<li class="block_16">Review the status on the current tasks, look for an imbalance in task assignment and who hasn’t started their tasks<br class="calibre2"/> </li>
<li class="block_16">You can still interact with tasks in the right column while viewing tasks, use the <b class="calibre6">Circle</b> at the top-right of the task card named <i class="calibre7">Test Samsung galaxy new model</i> to complete it<br class="calibre2"/> </li>
<li class="block_16">Note that this updates the charts<br class="calibre2"/><br class="calibre2"/><img alt="Image" class="calibre117" src="https://raw.githubusercontent.com/WebucatorTraining/skillable/main/55283/epub/images/image128.png"/></li>
<li class="block_16">At the top of the page, next to the name of the plan, <i class="calibre7">Hardware Refresh</i> click on <img alt="Star" class="calibre118" src="https://raw.githubusercontent.com/WebucatorTraining/skillable/main/55283/epub/images/image-43.png"/> <b class="calibre6">Add to favourites</b><br class="calibre2"/> </li>
<li class="block_16">Note that the plan now appears in the left navigation bar<br class="calibre2"/><br class="calibre2"/><img alt="Image" class="calibre119" src="https://raw.githubusercontent.com/WebucatorTraining/skillable/main/55283/epub/images/image131.png"/><br class="calibre2"/> </li>
<li class="block_26">At the top of the left navigation bar, click on <b class="calibre6">Planner hub</b> which your favourite plans are pinned to, as you gain access to more plans in your workplace, you can use this menu to access all your plans and pin your favourites to the top of the hub</li>
</ol>

# Exercise 1: Create a new Team 
<p class="block_">Your colleagues have started to use the IT Support SharePoint site but are looking for an area to chat to each other, share ideas, research, and collaborate with each other. As a content management system, SharePoint gives us a place to store and manage content however Teams is the place that pull this storage and other Microsoft 365 apps together. In this exercise we will add a Team to our existing Microsoft 365 Group.</p>
<ol class="list_">
<li class="block_15">Click on the <b class="calibre6">app launcher </b><img alt="Image" class="calibre15" src="https://raw.githubusercontent.com/WebucatorTraining/skillable/main/55283/epub/images/image-3.jpeg"/><b class="calibre6"> </b>and choose <b class="calibre6">Teams</b></li>
</ol>
<p class="block_27"><br class="calibre2"/><img alt="Image" class="calibre121" src="https://raw.githubusercontent.com/WebucatorTraining/skillable/main/55283/epub/images/image133.png"/><br class="calibre2"/> </p>
<p class="block_27">If you see a welcome message inviting you to ‘Download the Teams desktop app and stay better connected’ ignore the <i class="calibre7">Get the Windows app</i> option and select <b class="calibre6">Use the web app instead</b><br class="calibre2"/><br class="calibre2"/><img alt="Image" class="calibre122" src="https://raw.githubusercontent.com/WebucatorTraining/skillable/main/55283/epub/images/image134.png"/><br class="calibre2"/> </p>
<ol class="list_">
<li class="block_16" value="2">Click through the welcome pop-up then click <b class="calibre6">Let’s go</b><br class="calibre2"/> </li>
<li class="block_16">With the <i class="calibre7">Teams</i> tab selected on the left, at the bottom of the grey panel, click on <b class="calibre6">Join or create a team</b><br class="calibre2"/><br class="calibre2"/><img alt="Image" class="calibre123" src="https://raw.githubusercontent.com/WebucatorTraining/skillable/main/55283/epub/images/image-45.png"/></li>
<li class="block_16">Under <i class="calibre7">Create a Team</i>, click <b class="calibre6">Create team<br class="calibre2"/> </b></li>
</ol>
<p class="block_27"><img alt="Image" class="calibre124" src="https://raw.githubusercontent.com/WebucatorTraining/skillable/main/55283/epub/images/image136.png"/></p>
<ol class="list_">
<li class="block_16" value="5">Choose <b class="calibre6">From a group or team<br class="calibre2"/> </b></li>
<li class="block_16">Choose<b class="calibre6"> Microsoft 365 group<br class="calibre2"/> </b></li>
<li class="block_16">Select your Microsoft 365 group e.g. <b class="calibre6">Chris – IT Support</b> (note that it won’t highlight the group when you click it, even if there were more groups to pick from)</li>
</ol>
<p class="block_18"> </p>
<ol class="list_">
<li class="block_26" value="8">Click <b class="calibre6">Create</b></li>
</ol>

# Exercise 2 – Configure Team settings
<p class="block_18"> </p>
<ol class="list_">
<li class="block_16">Because the Team is based on our Microsoft 365 group, the correct audience already has access, however you may need to elect a colleague as an owner to help manage to team, to open the Team’s security settings click on the <b class="calibre6">ellipsis (…)</b> to the right of your Team’s name<br class="calibre2"/><br class="calibre2"/><img alt="Image" class="calibre125" src="https://raw.githubusercontent.com/WebucatorTraining/skillable/main/55283/epub/images/image-46.png"/></li>
</ol>
<p class="block_18"> </p>
<ol class="list_">
<li class="block_16" value="2">Select <b class="calibre6">Manage team</b> which will open on the <i class="calibre7">Members</i> tab<br class="calibre2"/> </li>
</ol>
<p class="block_18"> </p>
<ol class="list_">
<li class="block_16" value="3">Expand <b class="calibre6">Members and guests</b><br class="calibre2"/><br class="calibre2"/><img alt="Image" class="calibre126" src="https://raw.githubusercontent.com/WebucatorTraining/skillable/main/55283/epub/images/image138.png"/></li>
</ol>
<p class="block_18"> </p>
<ol class="list_">
<li class="block_16" value="4">Click on the <b class="calibre6">drop down</b> arrow to the right of <i class="calibre7">Caroline Lee<br class="calibre2"/><br class="calibre2"/></i><img alt="Image" class="calibre127" src="https://raw.githubusercontent.com/WebucatorTraining/skillable/main/55283/epub/images/image-47.png"/></li>
<li class="block_16">Choose <b class="calibre6">Owner</b> and Caroline will be moved into the <i class="calibre7">Owners</i> group where she can manage the team<br class="calibre2"/> </li>
<li class="block_16">You have had some experience in other teams where members have created unwanted channels and have filled feeds with posts full of GIFs and Memes which is hampering productivity, to change these settings click on the <b class="calibre6">Settings </b>tab (which may be in a sub menu)<br class="calibre2"/><br class="calibre2"/><img alt="Image" class="calibre128" src="https://raw.githubusercontent.com/WebucatorTraining/skillable/main/55283/epub/images/image140.png"/><br class="calibre2"/> </li>
<li class="block_16">Expand the <b class="calibre6">Member permissions</b><br class="calibre2"/> </li>
<li class="block_16">Untick:</li>
</ol>
<ol class="list_3">
<li class="block_28"><b class="calibre6">Allow members to create and update channels</b></li>
<li class="block_28"><b class="calibre6">Allow members to create private channels (disabled by previous selection)</b></li>
<li class="block_28"><b class="calibre6">Allow members to delete and restore channels</b></li>
<li class="block_28"><b class="calibre6">Allow members to add and remove apps</b></li>
<li class="block_28"><b class="calibre6">Allow members to upload custom apps</b><br class="calibre2"/> </li>
</ol>
<ol class="list_">
<li class="block_16" value="9"> Scroll down and expand <b class="calibre6">Fun stuff</b><br class="calibre2"/> </li>
<li class="block_16">Untick all the available options (do not worry we made you do this)<br class="calibre2"/> </li>
<li class="block_26">The team is now ready to receive channels</li>
</ol>

# Exercise 3: Add channels and tabs 
<p class="block_">You will now customise the team to help people find the content that you will upload. To do this we will introduce channels. These are areas for conversation, content and other apps that are related to these segmented areas. This will also leverage the SharePoint site in your Microsoft 365 group to store the files placed. The goal is to establish a structure to encourage other users to contribute content on specific topics in a structured way.</p>
<p class="block_">We will create channels for each team within the IT support department, for this example:</p>
<ul class="list_1">
<li class="block_45">IT Service Desk</li>
<li class="block_46">IT Service Delivery</li>
<li class="block_46">IT Service Development</li>
<li class="block_47">IT Budget [Private]</li>
</ul>
<p class="block_">To add each new Channel, follow these steps.</p>
<ol class="list_">
<li class="block_15">Click <b class="calibre6">ellipsis (…)</b> to the right of your Team’s name, then click <b class="calibre6">Add channel<br class="calibre2"/> </b></li>
</ol>
<p class="block_27"><img alt="Image" class="calibre129" src="https://raw.githubusercontent.com/WebucatorTraining/skillable/main/55283/epub/images/image-48.png"/><br class="calibre2"/> </p>
<ol class="list_">
<li class="block_16" value="2">Enter <b class="calibre6">IT Service Desk</b> as the channel name, do not enter anything in the description<br class="calibre2"/> </li>
<li class="block_23">Click <b class="calibre6">Add</b></li>
</ol>
<p class="block_48">Repeat steps 1 to 3 for each service in IT creating <b class="calibre6">IT Service Delivery</b> and <b class="calibre6">IT Service Development</b></p>
<ol class="list_">
<li class="block_15" value="4">Create one more channel and name it, <b class="calibre6">IT Budget</b> however, set the <i class="calibre7">Privacy</i> to <b class="calibre6">Private</b> </li>
</ol>
<p class="block_27"><br class="calibre2"/><img alt="Image" class="calibre130" src="https://raw.githubusercontent.com/WebucatorTraining/skillable/main/55283/epub/images/image142.png"/><br class="calibre2"/> </p>
<ol class="list_">
<li class="block_16" value="5">Click <b class="calibre6">Next</b> then add the following people into the <i class="calibre7">IT Budget</i> private channel</li>
</ol>
<ol class="list_3">
<li class="block_28">Caroline Lee</li>
<li class="block_28">Steve Smith<br class="calibre2"/> </li>
</ol>
<ol class="list_">
<li class="block_16" value="6">Click <b class="calibre6">Add</b> then use the <b class="calibre6">Member</b> drop down button to elect <i class="calibre7">Caroline Lee</i> as an <b class="calibre6">Owner</b> of the private channel<br class="calibre2"/> </li>
<li class="block_16">Click <b class="calibre6">Done</b>, now yourself, Steve and Caroline are able to see the content of this channel whereas the other in the team cannot, your channel structure should resemble the image below<br class="calibre2"/><br class="calibre2"/><img alt="Image" class="calibre131" src="https://raw.githubusercontent.com/WebucatorTraining/skillable/main/55283/epub/images/image143.png"/></li>
</ol>
<p class="block_18"> </p>
<ol class="list_">
<li class="block_16" value="8">To complement the functionality in the <i class="calibre7">IT Service Development</i> channel the team has asked for some useful assets, they need:</li>
</ol>
<ol class="list_3">
<li class="block_28">The plan that you set up for the hardware refresh</li>
<li class="block_28">The helpful links that were set up on your SharePoint home page<br class="calibre2"/> </li>
</ol>
<ol class="list_">
<li class="block_16" value="9">To achieve this, click on the <b class="calibre6">IT Service Development </b>channel<br class="calibre2"/> </li>
<li class="block_16">Click on the <b class="calibre6">Add a tab</b> button<b class="calibre6"><br class="calibre2"/><br class="calibre2"/></b><img alt="Image" class="calibre132" src="https://raw.githubusercontent.com/WebucatorTraining/skillable/main/55283/epub/images/image-49.png"/><br class="calibre2"/> </li>
<li class="block_16">Click <b class="calibre6">SharePoint Pages</b><br class="calibre2"/> </li>
<li class="block_16">Select <b class="calibre6">Home</b> then click <b class="calibre6">Save<br class="calibre2"/> </b></li>
<li class="block_16">Note that the tab is called <i class="calibre7">Home</i>, we can change this, click on the <b class="calibre6">drop down</b> arrow next to the <i class="calibre7">Home </i>tab<br class="calibre2"/><br class="calibre2"/><img alt="Image" class="calibre133" src="https://raw.githubusercontent.com/WebucatorTraining/skillable/main/55283/epub/images/image-50.png"/><br class="calibre2"/> </li>
<li class="block_16">Click<b class="calibre6"> Rename</b> and then change the name of the tab to <b class="calibre6">Our Site</b> then click <b class="calibre6">Save</b><br class="calibre2"/> </li>
<li class="block_16">To add your plan as a tab, click on the <b class="calibre6">Add a tab</b> button once more<br class="calibre2"/><br class="calibre2"/><img alt="Image" class="calibre134" src="https://raw.githubusercontent.com/WebucatorTraining/skillable/main/55283/epub/images/image-51.png"/><br class="calibre2"/> </li>
<li class="block_16">Select <b class="calibre6">Planner</b><br class="calibre2"/> </li>
<li class="block_16">Select the option <b class="calibre6">Use an existing plan form this team</b><br class="calibre2"/> </li>
<li class="block_16">Click on the drop down (currently listing <i class="calibre7">Existing plans</i>)<br class="calibre2"/><br class="calibre2"/><img alt="Image" class="calibre135" src="https://raw.githubusercontent.com/WebucatorTraining/skillable/main/55283/epub/images/image147.png"/></li>
<li class="block_16">Select <b class="calibre6">Hardware Refresh</b><br class="calibre2"/> </li>
<li class="block_16">Click <b class="calibre6">Save</b><br class="calibre2"/> </li>
<li class="block_16">The plan is now accessible from within this channel<br class="calibre2"/> </li>
<li class="block_26">Now that we have set up our team, we will now communicate within it</li>
</ol>

# Exercise 4: Chat within your Team
<p class="block_">You will now welcome your team by putting an announcement in the general channel. The general channel is a great place to post messages that are relevant to everyone whereas channels are best for more focused discussions. As the owner of the team you can control what non-members can do in the general channel, to avoid it becoming misused.</p>
<ol class="list_">
<li class="block_15">Within your Team, select the <b class="calibre6">General</b> channel<br class="calibre2"/> </li>
<li class="block_16">Click on the <b class="calibre6">New conversation </b>button<br class="calibre2"/><br class="calibre2"/><img alt="Image" class="calibre136" src="https://raw.githubusercontent.com/WebucatorTraining/skillable/main/55283/epub/images/image148.png"/><br class="calibre2"/> </li>
<li class="block_16">Click on the <b class="calibre6">Format</b> button as shown below<br class="calibre2"/><br class="calibre2"/><img alt="Image" class="calibre137" src="https://raw.githubusercontent.com/WebucatorTraining/skillable/main/55283/epub/images/image-52.png"/><br class="calibre2"/> </li>
<li class="block_16">Click on <b class="calibre6">New conversation</b> and then from the drop down menu choose <b class="calibre6">Announcement</b><br class="calibre2"/><br class="calibre2"/><img alt="Image" class="calibre138" src="https://raw.githubusercontent.com/WebucatorTraining/skillable/main/55283/epub/images/image-53.png"/><br class="calibre2"/> </li>
<li class="block_16">Enter a headline of <b class="calibre6">Welcome to our new Team!</b><br class="calibre2"/> </li>
<li class="block_16">Within the banner, click on the <b class="calibre6">Background Image </b>icon<br class="calibre2"/><br class="calibre2"/><img alt="Image" class="calibre139" src="https://raw.githubusercontent.com/WebucatorTraining/skillable/main/55283/epub/images/image-54.png"/></li>
<li class="block_16">Click on <b class="calibre6">Upload an image</b> and select any image from your computer to use in the banner then click <b class="calibre6">Open</b>, then <b class="calibre6">Done</b> (if you cannot find an image, you can use the <b class="calibre6">Color scheme</b> button to simply change the colour)<br class="calibre2"/><br class="calibre2"/><img alt="Image" class="calibre140" src="https://raw.githubusercontent.com/WebucatorTraining/skillable/main/55283/epub/images/image152.png"/><br class="calibre2"/> </li>
<li class="block_16">Below the banner click on <b class="calibre6">Add a subhead</b> and enter <b class="calibre6">Introducing new ways of working</b><br class="calibre2"/> </li>
<li class="block_16">To ensure that everyone gets a notification about this post we will @mention the name of the team which will notify all members, to do this, click into the body of the post as shown below<br class="calibre2"/><br class="calibre2"/><img alt="Image" class="calibre141" src="https://raw.githubusercontent.com/WebucatorTraining/skillable/main/55283/epub/images/image153.png"/></li>
<li class="block_16">Enter, <b class="calibre6">Thanks for everyone’s patience, we are happy that the new @</b> then after typing the @ character you are shown suggestions as shown below<br class="calibre2"/><br class="calibre2"/><img alt="Image" class="calibre142" src="https://raw.githubusercontent.com/WebucatorTraining/skillable/main/55283/epub/images/image154.png"/></li>
<li class="block_16">Immediately after the @ character enter the name of your team e.g. <b class="calibre6">Chris – IT Support</b><br class="calibre2"/> </li>
<li class="block_16">Finish the sentence after the @mention then continue with, <b class="calibre6">We hope you enjoy the new tools that are on offer here to help excel your productivity! </b></li>
</ol>
<p class="block_27">The result should resemble the following<br class="calibre2"/><br class="calibre2"/><img alt="Image" class="calibre143" src="https://raw.githubusercontent.com/WebucatorTraining/skillable/main/55283/epub/images/image155.png"/><br class="calibre2"/> </p>
<ol class="list_">
<li class="block_26" value="13">Click on the <b class="calibre6">Send</b><span class="calibre144"> </span><img alt="Image" class="calibre145" src="https://raw.githubusercontent.com/WebucatorTraining/skillable/main/55283/epub/images/image156.png"/> button to submit the post <br class="calibre2"/> </li>
</ol>

# Lab 7 – Working with videos using Steam
<p class="block_"><img alt="Graphical user interface, application  Description automatically generated" class="calibre120" src="https://raw.githubusercontent.com/WebucatorTraining/skillable/main/55283/epub/images/image-55.png"/></p>
<p class="block_">In this lab we will create a new channel for video content that is going to benefit the whole organisation. We will then upload a video to this channel and add properties to promote the videos content. We can then use these videos in other areas of Microsoft 365, helping others to steam corporate videos directly to their favourite apps.</p>

>[+] Exercise List (Click to Open)
> 1. [Activating Your Software for Class](#activating-your-software-for-class)
> 1. [Lab 2 – Managing content with OneDrive](#lab-2-–-managing-content-with-onedrive)
> 1. [Exercise 1 – Creating folders &amp; adding content](#exercise-1-–-creating-folders-&amp;-adding-content)
> 1. [Exercise 2 – Working with files](#exercise-2-–-working-with-files)
> 1. [Exercise 3 – Share a File](#exercise-3-–-share-a-file)
> 1. [Exercise 4 – Creating and deleting files](#exercise-4-–-creating-and-deleting-files)
> 1. [Exercise 5 - Sorting and viewing](#exercise-5---sorting-and-viewing)
> 1. [Lab 3 – Working with Apps](#lab-3-–-working-with-apps)
> 1. [Exercise 1 – Working with e-mail messages](#exercise-1-–-working-with-e-mail-messages)
> 1. [Exercise 2 – Working with calendars](#exercise-2-–-working-with-calendars)

# Exercise 1 – Create a new channel
<p class="block_">We will begin this lab by creating a new channel for our video content in Microsoft Stream.</p>
<ol class="list_">
<li class="block_15">In your Microsoft 365 tenant click on the <b class="calibre6">app launcher </b><img alt="Background pattern  Description automatically generated" class="calibre146" src="https://raw.githubusercontent.com/WebucatorTraining/skillable/main/55283/epub/images/image-4.jpeg"/> then select <b class="calibre6">All apps</b> then click on <b class="calibre6">Stream</b> <br class="calibre2"/><br class="calibre2"/><img alt="Image" class="calibre147" src="https://raw.githubusercontent.com/WebucatorTraining/skillable/main/55283/epub/images/image159.png"/></li>
</ol>
<ol class="list_">
<li class="block_16" value="2">Click on <b class="calibre6">+ Create</b> in the navigation toolbar at the top of the page and select <b class="calibre6">Channel<br class="calibre2"/> </b></li>
<li class="block_16">Give the Channel the name <b class="calibre6">[Your Name] - Training Videos</b> e.g. Chris – Training Videos<b class="calibre6"><br class="calibre2"/> </b></li>
<li class="block_16">Type the description Where we store all our Training videos for our team #Learning<br class="calibre2"/> </li>
<li class="block_16">Select the <b class="calibre6">Companywide channel</b> radio button<br class="calibre2"/> </li>
<li class="block_16">Click on the plus to add an image for the channel – choose <b class="calibre6">Community.jpg</b> from the <b class="calibre6">SPOnlineFiles </b>&gt; <b class="calibre6">Documents</b> folder of the download pack<br class="calibre2"/> </li>
<li class="block_16">Click <b class="calibre6">Create<br class="calibre2"/> </b></li>
<li class="block_26">Click on <b class="calibre6">Follow</b> which will change to following<b class="calibre6"><br class="calibre2"/><br class="calibre2"/></b><img alt="Image" class="calibre148" src="https://raw.githubusercontent.com/WebucatorTraining/skillable/main/55283/epub/images/image-56.png"/></li>
</ol>

# Exercise 2 – Add videos to a channel
<p class="block_">Next, we will associate our first video with this new channel.</p>
<ol class="list_">
<li class="block_15">Within the channel click on <b class="calibre6">select more files</b> <br class="calibre2"/><br class="calibre2"/><img alt="Image" class="calibre149" src="https://raw.githubusercontent.com/WebucatorTraining/skillable/main/55283/epub/images/image161.png"/><br class="calibre2"/> </li>
</ol>
<ol class="list_">
<li class="block_16" value="2">File explorer will open, navigate to your course download pack on your computer and open the folder <b class="calibre6">SPOnlineFiles</b> &gt; <b class="calibre6">Page files</b> folder and find <b class="calibre6">Training on demand.mp4<br class="calibre2"/> </b></li>
<li class="block_16">Click <b class="calibre6">Open<br class="calibre2"/> </b></li>
<li class="block_16"><b class="calibre6">Select </b>English as the video language and click <b class="calibre6">Save<br class="calibre2"/> </b></li>
<li class="block_16">Keep the name as <b class="calibre6">Training on demand<br class="calibre2"/> </b></li>
<li class="block_16">Set the language as <b class="calibre6">English</b> then click <b class="calibre6">Save</b><br class="calibre2"/> </li>
<li class="block_16">On the next page, add a description – <b class="calibre6">Learn on-demand at any time within Microsoft 365</b>.<br class="calibre2"/> </li>
<li class="block_16">Change the Thumbnail to be the man standing in front of a presentation<br class="calibre2"/> </li>
<li class="block_16">Keep <i class="calibre7">Permissions</i> as the default – <b class="calibre6">Allow everyone in your company to view this video<br class="calibre2"/> </b></li>
<li class="block_23">Keep <i class="calibre7">Options</i> keep as they are</li>
</ol>
<p class="block_24"><img alt="Image" class="calibre150" src="https://raw.githubusercontent.com/WebucatorTraining/skillable/main/55283/epub/images/image162.png"/></p>
<ol class="list_">
<li class="block_15" value="11">Once uploaded click <b class="calibre6">Publish</b><br class="calibre2"/> </li>
<li class="block_16">In the top navigation bar click on <b class="calibre6">Discover</b> then <b class="calibre6">Channels</b><br class="calibre2"/> </li>
<li class="block_16">Click on your new channel<br class="calibre2"/> </li>
<li class="block_16">To the right of your video, click on <b class="calibre6">Add to watch list</b> (see below) which pins the video to your watchlist to return to later, the watchlist is found in the <i class="calibre7">My content</i> menu in the toolbar<br class="calibre2"/><br class="calibre2"/><img alt="Image" class="calibre151" src="https://raw.githubusercontent.com/WebucatorTraining/skillable/main/55283/epub/images/image-57.png"/></li>
<li class="block_16">Next, click on the video you uploaded<br class="calibre2"/> </li>
<li class="block_16">The video will play automatically, note that the video has no audio (we did this as you may be in an open office environment)<br class="calibre2"/> </li>
<li class="block_26">Leave this video open as we will want to share this content with our colleagues in Microsoft Teams<br class="calibre2"/> </li>
</ol>

# Exercise 3 – Share a video
<p class="block_">Normally to share a video we would use the videos link. Commonly we would paste the link into supported areas like Sway cards, SharePoint web parts or associate the link with entries in documents, chats, and web pages. We will discuss how to obtain this link and then we will use this link to add the video to a post in a Teams channel. We will then look at other ways to share a video in Teams.</p>
<ol class="list_">
<li class="block_15">Below the video are the videos details, click on the <b class="calibre6">Share</b> <img alt="Share" class="calibre118" src="https://raw.githubusercontent.com/WebucatorTraining/skillable/main/55283/epub/images/image-13.png"/> button<br class="calibre2"/><br class="calibre2"/><img alt="Image" class="calibre152" src="https://raw.githubusercontent.com/WebucatorTraining/skillable/main/55283/epub/images/image-58.png"/><br class="calibre2"/> </li>
</ol>
<ol class="list_">
<li class="block_16" value="2">In the pop-up window, to the right of the field titled <i class="calibre7">Direct link to video</i> click on <b class="calibre6">Copy</b><br class="calibre2"/><br class="calibre2"/><img alt="Image" class="calibre153" src="https://raw.githubusercontent.com/WebucatorTraining/skillable/main/55283/epub/images/image165.png"/></li>
<li class="block_16">The link is copied to your clipboard, click <b class="calibre6">Close</b> at the bottom of the pop-up window<br class="calibre2"/> </li>
<li class="block_16">In the <b class="calibre6">app launcher</b> <img alt="Background pattern  Description automatically generated" class="calibre154" src="https://raw.githubusercontent.com/WebucatorTraining/skillable/main/55283/epub/images/image-5.jpeg"/> select <b class="calibre6">Teams</b> (if asked, use the web browser version)<br class="calibre2"/> </li>
<li class="block_16">The <b class="calibre6">Teams</b> button should be highlighted in the left menu (if not, select <b class="calibre6">Teams</b>)<br class="calibre2"/> </li>
<li class="block_16">Within the <i class="calibre7">[Your name] – IT Support</i> team, select the <b class="calibre6">General</b> channel which should show the posts tab, if not select the <b class="calibre6">Posts</b> tab<br class="calibre2"/><br class="calibre2"/><img alt="Image" class="calibre155" src="https://raw.githubusercontent.com/WebucatorTraining/skillable/main/55283/epub/images/image167.png"/><br class="calibre2"/> </li>
<li class="block_16">Click <b class="calibre6">New conversation</b><br class="calibre2"/><br class="calibre2"/><img alt="Image" class="calibre156" src="https://raw.githubusercontent.com/WebucatorTraining/skillable/main/55283/epub/images/image-59.png"/></li>
<li class="block_16">Click on the <b class="calibre6">Format</b> button below the post<br class="calibre2"/><br class="calibre2"/><img alt="Image" class="calibre157" src="https://raw.githubusercontent.com/WebucatorTraining/skillable/main/55283/epub/images/image-60.png"/></li>
<li class="block_16">In the <i class="calibre7">Add a subject</i> section enter <b class="calibre6">Learn on-demand</b><br class="calibre2"/> </li>
<li class="block_16">In the body of the conversation enter, learn more about Microsoft 365 in this training video<br class="calibre2"/> </li>
<li class="block_16">Using your mouse, highlight the words <i class="calibre7">training video</i> in the body as shown below<br class="calibre2"/><br class="calibre2"/><img alt="Image" class="calibre158" src="https://raw.githubusercontent.com/WebucatorTraining/skillable/main/55283/epub/images/image170.png"/><br class="calibre2"/> </li>
<li class="block_16">On your keyboard press <b class="calibre6">CTRL</b> + <b class="calibre6">K</b> at the same time to open the hyperlink shortcut<br class="calibre2"/> </li>
<li class="block_16">Use <b class="calibre6">CTRL</b> + <b class="calibre6">V</b> at the same time to paste in your video link<br class="calibre2"/><br class="calibre2"/><img alt="Image" class="calibre159" src="https://raw.githubusercontent.com/WebucatorTraining/skillable/main/55283/epub/images/image171.png"/></li>
<li class="block_16">Click <b class="calibre6">Insert</b> then on the message click <b class="calibre6">Send</b> <img alt="Image" class="calibre160" src="https://raw.githubusercontent.com/WebucatorTraining/skillable/main/55283/epub/images/image172.png"/><br class="calibre2"/> </li>
<li class="block_16">Your colleague informs you that this video is very useful and it would be great to add the Stream channel as a tab so that any new videos can be accessed within the Team, within the <i class="calibre7">General</i> channel, click on <b class="calibre6">Add a tab</b><br class="calibre2"/><br class="calibre2"/><img alt="Image" class="calibre161" src="https://raw.githubusercontent.com/WebucatorTraining/skillable/main/55283/epub/images/image-61.png"/><br class="calibre2"/> </li>
<li class="block_16">Select <b class="calibre6">Stream</b><br class="calibre2"/> </li>
<li class="block_16">The <i class="calibre7">Channel </i>radio button is selected by default, in the Search field, enter the name of your Stream channel e.g. <b class="calibre6">Chris – Training Videos</b><br class="calibre2"/><br class="calibre2"/><img alt="Image" class="calibre162" src="https://raw.githubusercontent.com/WebucatorTraining/skillable/main/55283/epub/images/image174.png"/><br class="calibre2"/> </li>
<li class="block_16">Change the <i class="calibre7">Tab name</i> to <b class="calibre6">Training Videos </b>then<b class="calibre6"> </b>click<b class="calibre6"> Save</b><br class="calibre2"/> </li>
<li class="block_23">Your channel and video content will be presented within its own tab within Teams</li>
</ol>
<p class="block_39"> </p>

# Lab 8 – Create a Sway and a Yammer community
<p class="block_"><img alt="Image" class="calibre4" src="https://raw.githubusercontent.com/WebucatorTraining/skillable/main/55283/epub/images/image175.png"/></p>
<p class="block_">In this lab we will focus on creating a new Sway using a theme and content of your own choosing as well as start a new Yammer group for your Microsoft 365 Champion network.</p>

# Exercise 1 – Start a new Sway and add cards
<p class="block_">In this exercise we will begin by creating a new Sway and introduce some cards to showcase some engaging content for your colleagues.</p>
<ol class="list_">
<li class="block_15">From where we last worked in Teams, click on the <b class="calibre6">app launcher </b><img alt="Image" class="calibre15" src="https://raw.githubusercontent.com/WebucatorTraining/skillable/main/55283/epub/images/image.jpeg"/>, then choose <b class="calibre6">Microsoft 365<br class="calibre2"/></b><br class="calibre2"/><img alt="Image" class="calibre163" src="https://raw.githubusercontent.com/WebucatorTraining/skillable/main/55283/epub/images/image176.png"/></li>
<li class="block_16"> In the new browser tab, click on the <b class="calibre6">app launcher </b><img alt="Image" class="calibre15" src="https://raw.githubusercontent.com/WebucatorTraining/skillable/main/55283/epub/images/image.jpeg"/>, then <b class="calibre6">all apps</b> then select <b class="calibre6">Sway</b><br class="calibre2"/> </li>
<li class="block_16">On the Sway home page, click on <b class="calibre6">New blank Sway</b><br class="calibre2"/> </li>
<li class="block_16">This is your choice now, you are building this Sway, enter in the title of your Sway e.g. Dinosaurs, West Bromwich Albion, Tigers Japan, etc.<br class="calibre2"/><br class="calibre2"/><img alt="Image" class="calibre164" src="https://raw.githubusercontent.com/WebucatorTraining/skillable/main/55283/epub/images/image177.png"/><br class="calibre2"/> </li>
<li class="block_16">Click on the <b class="calibre6">Background</b> panel, within the <i class="calibre7">Title</i> card (see section to left in image above)<br class="calibre2"/> </li>
<li class="block_16">At the top of the content panel to the right, enter in a search term related to the subject of your Sway, then select a valid image, then click <b class="calibre6">Add</b><br class="calibre2"/><br class="calibre2"/><img alt="Image" class="calibre165" src="https://raw.githubusercontent.com/WebucatorTraining/skillable/main/55283/epub/images/image178.png"/><br class="calibre2"/> </li>
<li class="block_16">To add a new card, hover your mouse cursor below the <i class="calibre7">Title</i> card and click once, this opens the card menu<br class="calibre2"/><br class="calibre2"/><img alt="Image" class="calibre166" src="https://raw.githubusercontent.com/WebucatorTraining/skillable/main/55283/epub/images/image179.png"/></li>
<li class="block_16">Click on <b class="calibre6">Text<br class="calibre2"/> </b></li>
<li class="block_16">In the text card, enter some information around your subject matter, you can always copy and paste some text from another web page like Wikipedia<br class="calibre2"/> </li>
<li class="block_16">Below the text card, click on the <b class="calibre6">(+)</b> to add another picture using what you learned earlier when adding a background<br class="calibre2"/> </li>
<li class="block_16">In the image card, add a caption<br class="calibre2"/><br class="calibre2"/><img alt="Image" class="calibre167" src="https://raw.githubusercontent.com/WebucatorTraining/skillable/main/55283/epub/images/image180.png"/></li>
<li class="block_16">Click on the <b class="calibre6">(+)</b> below the new image card and choose the <b class="calibre6">Media</b> heading then choose <b class="calibre6">Video</b><br class="calibre2"/> </li>
<li class="block_16">Your search field may be pre-populated, you can change this search term if you want to, once ready, pick a video by selecting it then choose <b class="calibre6">Add<br class="calibre2"/> </b></li>
<li class="block_16">Again, add a caption for the video<br class="calibre2"/> </li>
<li class="block_23">Lastly, spend 2-3 minutes adding some new content to the Sway, you can drag and drop cards to move them around or even group them, once ready, move onto the next exercise</li>
</ol>
<p class="block_1"> </p>

# Exercise 2 – Change the design of the Sway
<p class="block_">Next you will check the visual experience of your Sway and change the way it looks and flows.</p>
<ol class="list_">
<li class="block_15">At the top of the Storyline you are currently building you will see another tab called <b class="calibre6">Design</b>, click on this tab<br class="calibre2"/><br class="calibre2"/><img alt="Image" class="calibre168" src="https://raw.githubusercontent.com/WebucatorTraining/skillable/main/55283/epub/images/image-62.png"/><br class="calibre2"/> </li>
<li class="block_16">Take a moment to use the <b class="calibre6">Left</b>, <b class="calibre6">Right</b> arrows at the bottom of the page to get a feel for the look of your content<br class="calibre2"/> </li>
<li class="block_16">Next, click on the <b class="calibre6">Styles</b> button at the top-right of the page<br class="calibre2"/><br class="calibre2"/><img alt="Image" class="calibre169" src="https://raw.githubusercontent.com/WebucatorTraining/skillable/main/55283/epub/images/image-63.png"/></li>
<li class="block_16">In the <i class="calibre7">Styles</i> pane, change the scrolling to <b class="calibre6">Vertical</b> or <b class="calibre6">Horizontal</b>, using your scroll wheel on your mouse to test the change, try the <b class="calibre6">Slides</b> option too then switch to your favourite<br class="calibre2"/> </li>
<li class="block_16">Next, choose the theme, you can do this by picking a theme from the selection below, customising the existing theme or choosing Remix at the top to randomly generate the theme, there is an <b class="calibre6">Undo</b> button at the top-right of the page<br class="calibre2"/><br class="calibre2"/><img alt="Image" class="calibre170" src="https://raw.githubusercontent.com/WebucatorTraining/skillable/main/55283/epub/images/image183.png"/><br class="calibre2"/> </li>
<li class="block_26">Once ready, leave your Sway open for the next exercise</li>
</ol>

# Exercise 3 – Share your Sway
<p class="block_">In this exercise you will share your Sway with a member of your communications team who will feature your Sway in a newsletter via a link</p>
<ol class="list_">
<li class="block_15">At the top-right of the page, click on <b class="calibre6">Share</b><br class="calibre2"/><br class="calibre2"/><img alt="Image" class="calibre171" src="https://raw.githubusercontent.com/WebucatorTraining/skillable/main/55283/epub/images/image184.png"/><br class="calibre2"/> </li>
<li class="block_16">So that the content in your Sway is only visible to people in your organisation, ensure that <b class="calibre6">Those in your organisation with this link</b> is selected<br class="calibre2"/> </li>
<li class="block_16">So that this audience can’t edit your Sway, ensure that <b class="calibre6">view</b> is selected<br class="calibre2"/> </li>
<li class="block_16">Next, click on <b class="calibre6">Get visual link</b> <br class="calibre2"/> </li>
<li class="block_16">In the visual link preview, choose <b class="calibre6">Copy</b><br class="calibre2"/> </li>
<li class="block_16">Next click <b class="calibre6">Close<br class="calibre2"/><br class="calibre2"/></b><img alt="Image" class="calibre172" src="https://raw.githubusercontent.com/WebucatorTraining/skillable/main/55283/epub/images/image185.png"/><b class="calibre6"><br class="calibre2"/> </b></li>
<li class="block_16">Click on the <b class="calibre6">app launcher</b> <img alt="Image" class="calibre15" src="https://raw.githubusercontent.com/WebucatorTraining/skillable/main/55283/epub/images/image.jpeg"/>, from Sway this will open a new tab, then click on the <b class="calibre6">app launcher </b>again and choose <b class="calibre6">Outlook<br class="calibre2"/> </b></li>
<li class="block_16">Click on <b class="calibre6">+ New message</b><br class="calibre2"/> </li>
<li class="block_16">In the <i class="calibre7">To</i> field enter <b class="calibre6">Steve Smith</b><br class="calibre2"/> </li>
<li class="block_16">In the <i class="calibre7">Subject</i> enter, My newsletter content<br class="calibre2"/> </li>
<li class="block_16">In the <i class="calibre7">Body</i> paste the content you copied from Sway<br class="calibre2"/><br class="calibre2"/><img alt="Image" class="calibre173" src="https://raw.githubusercontent.com/WebucatorTraining/skillable/main/55283/epub/images/image186.png"/><br class="calibre2"/> </li>
<li class="block_23">Once ready, click <b class="calibre6">Send</b></li>
</ol>
<p class="block_1"> </p>

# Exercise 4 – Create a new Yammer group
<p class="block_">In this exercise we will set up a new Yammer group for our Microsoft 365 champions’ network. We will invite some of our existing champions into the group and configure it so that it is discoverable by other staff.</p>
<ol class="list_">
<li class="block_15">Click on the <b class="calibre6">app launcher</b> <img alt="Image" class="calibre15" src="https://raw.githubusercontent.com/WebucatorTraining/skillable/main/55283/epub/images/image.jpeg"/>, then choose <b class="calibre6">Yammer</b><br class="calibre2"/> </li>
<li class="block_23">In the left navigation under <i class="calibre7">My communities</i>, click on the <b class="calibre6">Create a Community</b> option </li>
</ol>
<table class="table_1">
<tbody class="calibre67"><tr class="calibre68">
<td class="td_6"><p class="block_38"><img alt="Image" class="calibre174" src="https://raw.githubusercontent.com/WebucatorTraining/skillable/main/55283/epub/images/image187.png"/></p></td>
<td class="td_7"><p class="block_38">If your interface does not look like the image to the left, you may be using an older interface for Yammer. If this is the case there is a toggle at the top of the page to switch to the new Yammer interface, Once this is turned on, your interface should match the steps in this exercise.</p></td>
</tr>
</tbody></table>
<p class="block_18"> </p>
<ol class="list_">
<li class="block_16" value="3">Enter in the community name <b class="calibre6">[Your Name] – Microsoft 365 Champions </b>e.g. Chris – Microsoft 365 Champions<br class="calibre2"/> </li>
<li class="block_16">Ignore group members for now, we may need to invite our colleagues to Yammer if they are not using it yet<br class="calibre2"/> </li>
<li class="block_16">Ensure that the privacy is set to <b class="calibre6">Public Access</b> so that your colleagues can see the community when they eventually join Yammer<br class="calibre2"/> </li>
<li class="block_16">Click <b class="calibre6">Create </b>which is at the bottom right of the settings menu<br class="calibre2"/> </li>
<li class="block_16">Click on the <b class="calibre6">ellipsis (…)</b> to the right of your community name then from the menu choose <b class="calibre6">Settings</b> <br class="calibre2"/><br class="calibre2"/><img alt="Image" class="calibre175" src="https://raw.githubusercontent.com/WebucatorTraining/skillable/main/55283/epub/images/image188.png"/><br class="calibre2"/> </li>
<li class="block_16">Below the Image, click <b class="calibre6">Add</b><br class="calibre2"/><br class="calibre2"/><img alt="Image" class="calibre176" src="https://raw.githubusercontent.com/WebucatorTraining/skillable/main/55283/epub/images/image189.png"/></li>
<li class="block_16">In the download pack, open the <b class="calibre6">Branding </b>folder and select <b class="calibre6">House Rules Slogan.png</b> and click <b class="calibre6">Open</b><br class="calibre2"/> </li>
<li class="block_16">Scroll down and change <i class="calibre7">DEFAULT PUBLISHER TYPE</i> to <b class="calibre6">Question</b>, then click <b class="calibre6">Save changes</b><br class="calibre2"/><br class="calibre2"/>Move your mouse cursor over the cover photo at the top of the community and click <b class="calibre6">Update Cover Photo</b> &gt; <b class="calibre6">Upload Cover Photo</b><br class="calibre2"/><br class="calibre2"/><img alt="Image" class="calibre177" src="https://raw.githubusercontent.com/WebucatorTraining/skillable/main/55283/epub/images/image190.png"/><br class="calibre2"/> </li>
<li class="block_16">Select the file <b class="calibre6">House Rules Gaming</b> from the <i class="calibre7">Branding </i>folder of the download pack and click <b class="calibre6">Open</b><br class="calibre2"/><br class="calibre2"/><img alt="Image" class="calibre178" src="https://raw.githubusercontent.com/WebucatorTraining/skillable/main/55283/epub/images/image191.png"/><br class="calibre2"/> </li>
<li class="block_16">Optionally, add a description e.g. </li>
</ol>
<p class="block_18"> </p>
<p class="block_27">This group is managed by our Microsoft 365 champions are here to support various departments with their continued adoption of these services.<br class="calibre2"/> </p>
<ol class="list_">
<li class="block_16" value="13">At the bottom of the page click <b class="calibre6">Save Changes</b><br class="calibre2"/> </li>
<li class="block_16">Click in the section titled <b class="calibre6">Share something with this community</b><br class="calibre2"/><br class="calibre2"/><img alt="Image" class="calibre179" src="https://raw.githubusercontent.com/WebucatorTraining/skillable/main/55283/epub/images/image192.png"/><br class="calibre2"/> </li>
<li class="block_16">Enter into the conversation: <b class="calibre6">We would like to welcome all our champions to this community. This is a public area where people can ask our champions questions and share their passion for Microsoft 365.</b><br class="calibre2"/> </li>
<li class="block_16">Click <b class="calibre6">Post</b><br class="calibre2"/> </li>
<li class="block_26">Now that the community is set up as a public area, anyone in Yammer can join this group, ask questions, and follow the conversations<br class="calibre2"/> </li>
</ol>

# Lab 9 – Building a custom time off solution
<p class="block_"><img alt="Image" class="calibre120" src="https://raw.githubusercontent.com/WebucatorTraining/skillable/main/55283/epub/images/image193.png"/></p>
<p class="block_">In this lab we will be attempting to resolve an issue with our historic time off request process. At the moment, time off requests are logged in an Excel spreadsheet. Any new requests need to be signed off by a line manager. At present, when the spreadsheet is updated, the requestee must email or talk to their line manager to request they approve the time off. Most parties involved in the process are not satisfied with the degree of manual work required to push this process along as well as the lack of mobility and reporting.</p>
<p class="block_22" id="calibre_pb_14">You have been asked to build a proof of concept for a new holiday request tool. You will be designing the new solution in Microsoft 365, making use of Power BI for reporting on the old Excel file, PowerApps for submitting requests and viewing reports and Flow for automating the approval process.</p>

# Exercise 1 – Create a time off report
<p class="block_">Although we are planning on designing a new solution for booking holidays, the old data still holds some value. We will use a table in the spreadsheet to report on locations visited and total time off per month.</p>
<ol class="list_">
<li class="block_15">In Microsoft 365, click the <b class="calibre6">app launcher</b> <img alt="Image" class="calibre15" src="https://raw.githubusercontent.com/WebucatorTraining/skillable/main/55283/epub/images/image.jpeg"/> then click on <b class="calibre6">All apps -&gt;</b> and click <b class="calibre6">Power BI<br class="calibre2"/><br class="calibre2"/></b><img alt="Image" class="calibre180" src="https://raw.githubusercontent.com/WebucatorTraining/skillable/main/55283/epub/images/image194.png"/><b class="calibre6"><br class="calibre2"/> </b></li>
<li class="block_16">The left navigation can be black (the old look) or white (the new look), if the look is white, continue to step 3, if not, click on <b class="calibre6">New look off</b> at the top of the page, to toggle the new look on<br class="calibre2"/><br class="calibre2"/><img alt="Image" class="calibre181" src="https://raw.githubusercontent.com/WebucatorTraining/skillable/main/55283/epub/images/image195.png"/><b class="calibre6"><br class="calibre2"/> </b></li>
<li class="block_16">In the left navigation, click <b class="calibre6">My Workspace</b> to open your personal work area in Power BI<br class="calibre2"/><br class="calibre2"/><img alt="Image" class="calibre182" src="https://raw.githubusercontent.com/WebucatorTraining/skillable/main/55283/epub/images/image196.png"/><br class="calibre2"/> </li>
<li class="block_16">With your workspace selected (indicated by a yellow tab to the left of the workspace name) click on the <b class="calibre6">Get data</b> button at the bottom left of the page<b class="calibre6"><br class="calibre2"/> </b></li>
<li class="block_16">Under the heading <i class="calibre7">Files</i><span class="text_8"> </span>choose the option <b class="calibre6">Get </b>(see following page)<br class="calibre2"/><br class="calibre2"/><img alt="Image" class="calibre183" src="https://raw.githubusercontent.com/WebucatorTraining/skillable/main/55283/epub/images/image197.png"/><br class="calibre2"/> </li>
<li class="block_16">In the menu, choose <b class="calibre6">Local File</b><br class="calibre2"/> </li>
<li class="block_16">From your course download pack, and navigate to <b class="calibre6">SPOnline Files </b>&gt; <b class="calibre6">Power Apps</b> and select <b class="calibre6">Holiday Requests</b> then click <b class="calibre6">Open</b><br class="calibre2"/> </li>
<li class="block_16">Choose the option to <b class="calibre6">Import </b>when asked how to connect to your Excel workbook<b class="calibre6"><br class="calibre2"/><br class="calibre2"/></b><img alt="Image" class="calibre184" src="https://raw.githubusercontent.com/WebucatorTraining/skillable/main/55283/epub/images/image198.png"/><b class="calibre6"><br class="calibre2"/> </b></li>
<li class="block_16">Once the dataset is ready, expand your <b class="calibre6">My Workspace</b> in the left navigation and under the heading <i class="calibre7">Datasets</i> click on <b class="calibre6">Holiday Requests</b><br class="calibre2"/><br class="calibre2"/><img alt="Image" class="calibre185" src="https://raw.githubusercontent.com/WebucatorTraining/skillable/main/55283/epub/images/image199.png"/><br class="calibre2"/> </li>
</ol>
<p class="block_18"> </p>
<ol class="list_">
<li class="block_16" value="10">On the report designer, review the options available in the <i class="calibre7">Visualizations </i>pane then choose <b class="calibre6">Map </b>(consider collapsing the <i class="calibre7">Filters</i> pane to gain more space on the page)<br class="calibre2"/><br class="calibre2"/><img alt="Image" class="calibre186" src="https://raw.githubusercontent.com/WebucatorTraining/skillable/main/55283/epub/images/image200.png"/><br class="calibre2"/> </li>
<li class="block_16">Using the resizing handle, stretch the visualisation so that it is wider (you don’t need to fill the page)<br class="calibre2"/><br class="calibre2"/><img alt="Image" class="calibre187" src="https://raw.githubusercontent.com/WebucatorTraining/skillable/main/55283/epub/images/image201.png"/><br class="calibre2"/> </li>
<li class="block_16">Drag the <b class="calibre6">Location</b> column from the <i class="calibre7">Fields</i> pane into the <i class="calibre7">Location</i> well for the map visualization (be patient when dragging and dropping, the interface can lag)<br class="calibre2"/><br class="calibre2"/><img alt="Image" class="calibre188" src="https://raw.githubusercontent.com/WebucatorTraining/skillable/main/55283/epub/images/image202.png"/><br class="calibre2"/> </li>
<li class="block_16">Next, click on the white space below the map visual*, then in the <i class="calibre7">Visualizations</i> pane, choose <b class="calibre6">Ribbon chart </b>(*If you leave the map selected and click another visual, you will end up changing the map to the new visual, if you accidently do this, click on <b class="calibre6">Map</b> again with the visual selected)<br class="calibre2"/><br class="calibre2"/><img alt="Image" class="calibre189" src="https://raw.githubusercontent.com/WebucatorTraining/skillable/main/55283/epub/images/image203.png"/><br class="calibre2"/> </li>
<li class="block_16">Drag the following columns from the <i class="calibre7">Fields</i> pane into the wells for the selected ribbon chart visual (this will show the flow of number of days booked of by staff by year)<br class="calibre2"/><br class="calibre2"/><img alt="Image" class="calibre190" src="https://raw.githubusercontent.com/WebucatorTraining/skillable/main/55283/epub/images/image204.png"/><br class="calibre2"/> </li>
<li class="block_16">Resize the visual, to allow for some space to its right as shown on the next page (remember to be patient when dragging and dropping)<br class="calibre2"/><br class="calibre2"/><img alt="Image" class="calibre191" src="https://raw.githubusercontent.com/WebucatorTraining/skillable/main/55283/epub/images/image205.png"/><br class="calibre2"/> </li>
<li class="block_16">Click into the space you have made and from the <i class="calibre7">visualization</i> pane, add the <b class="calibre6">Slicer</b> visual (remember that you need to deselect a visual before adding another)<br class="calibre2"/><br class="calibre2"/><img alt="Image" class="calibre192" src="https://raw.githubusercontent.com/WebucatorTraining/skillable/main/55283/epub/images/image206.png"/><br class="calibre2"/> </li>
<li class="block_16">It should fit into the gap but adjust it if required, and with the visual selected, drag the <b class="calibre6">Name</b> field into the <i class="calibre7">Field</i> well<br class="calibre2"/><br class="calibre2"/><img alt="Image" class="calibre193" src="https://raw.githubusercontent.com/WebucatorTraining/skillable/main/55283/epub/images/image-64.png"/><br class="calibre2"/> </li>
<li class="block_16">To make the slicer easier to use, click on the <b class="calibre6">Format </b><img alt="Image" class="calibre194" src="https://raw.githubusercontent.com/WebucatorTraining/skillable/main/55283/epub/images/image208.png"/><b class="calibre6"> </b>button then expand the <b class="calibre6">General</b> option, changing the <i class="calibre7">Orientation</i> to <b class="calibre6">Horizontal</b><br class="calibre2"/><br class="calibre2"/><img alt="Image" class="calibre195" src="https://raw.githubusercontent.com/WebucatorTraining/skillable/main/55283/epub/images/image209.png"/><br class="calibre2"/> </li>
<li class="block_16">The slicer will appear as tiles, click on a member of staff to filter the current visuals on the page, click on it again to undo the filter<br class="calibre2"/><br class="calibre2"/><img alt="Image" class="calibre196" src="https://raw.githubusercontent.com/WebucatorTraining/skillable/main/55283/epub/images/image210.png"/><br class="calibre2"/> </li>
<li class="block_16">Finally, right click on the tab titled <i class="calibre7">Page 1</i> at the bottom left of the report and choose <b class="calibre6">Rename Page<br class="calibre2"/><br class="calibre2"/></b><img alt="Image" class="calibre197" src="https://raw.githubusercontent.com/WebucatorTraining/skillable/main/55283/epub/images/image211.png"/><br class="calibre2"/> </li>
<li class="block_16">Name the page ‘Holiday by year and location’<br class="calibre2"/> </li>
<li class="block_16">Then click on the <b class="calibre6">File</b> button at the top of the page and choose <b class="calibre6">Save</b><br class="calibre2"/><br class="calibre2"/><img alt="Image" class="calibre198" src="https://raw.githubusercontent.com/WebucatorTraining/skillable/main/55283/epub/images/image-65.png"/><br class="calibre2"/> </li>
<li class="block_23">Name the report ‘Holiday Report’ then click <b class="calibre6">Save</b><br class="calibre2"/> </li>
</ol>
<p class="block_">Your report should resemble the following:<br class="calibre2"/><br class="calibre2"/><img alt="Image" class="calibre199" src="https://raw.githubusercontent.com/WebucatorTraining/skillable/main/55283/epub/images/image213.png"/></p>
<ol class="list_">
<li class="block_15" value="24">In the left navigation, click on the drop-down arrow next to <b class="calibre6">My Workspace </b>to expand this workspace, click on <b class="calibre6">Holiday Report </b>under the <i class="calibre7">Reports</i> heading (note that it may already be selected)<br class="calibre2"/><br class="calibre2"/><img alt="Image" class="calibre200" src="https://raw.githubusercontent.com/WebucatorTraining/skillable/main/55283/epub/images/image214.png"/><br class="calibre2"/> </li>
<li class="block_16">Hover your mouse cursor over the top visualisation and a pin will appear at the top right of the visualisation, click on this <b class="calibre6">Pin</b> (the toolbar may generate in a different location to the one in the image below)<br class="calibre2"/><br class="calibre2"/><img alt="Image" class="calibre201" src="https://raw.githubusercontent.com/WebucatorTraining/skillable/main/55283/epub/images/image-66.png"/></li>
<li class="block_16">Ensure the <i class="calibre7">Holiday Requests.xlsx</i> dashboard is selected and choose <b class="calibre6">Pin </b><br class="calibre2"/> </li>
<li class="block_16">Repeat step 25 for the bottom ribbon chart visualisation<br class="calibre2"/> </li>
<li class="block_16">In the left navigation in <i class="calibre7">My Workspace</i> under <i class="calibre7">Dashboards</i> hover your mouse over <b class="calibre6">Holiday Dashboard.xlsx</b>, select the <b class="calibre6">ellipsis (…) </b>and choose <b class="calibre6">Rename </b><br class="calibre2"/> </li>
<li class="block_16">Name the dashboard ‘Holiday Summary’ and press <b class="calibre6">Enter</b> on your keyboard<br class="calibre2"/> </li>
<li class="block_16">To pad out our dashboard further, we will use a tool called quick insights to generate a few more visuals, in your workspace menu, scroll down to your <i class="calibre7">Datasets</i> and click on the <b class="calibre6">ellipsis (…)</b> next to the <i class="calibre7">Holiday Requests </i>dataset (you will need to position your mouse cursor over Holiday Requests to display the ellipsis) then choose <b class="calibre6">Get quick insights</b> (see the next page)<br class="calibre2"/><br class="calibre2"/><img alt="Image" class="calibre202" src="https://raw.githubusercontent.com/WebucatorTraining/skillable/main/55283/epub/images/image216.png"/><br class="calibre2"/> </li>
<li class="block_16">Once ready, click on <b class="calibre6">View insights </b>(if you dismissed this message, repeat step 30)<br class="calibre2"/><br class="calibre2"/><img alt="Image" class="calibre203" src="https://raw.githubusercontent.com/WebucatorTraining/skillable/main/55283/epub/images/image-67.png"/><br class="calibre2"/> </li>
<li class="block_16">Scroll though the visualisations that have been generated by quick insights and use the <b class="calibre6">Pin</b> icon to add the ones you like to your dashboard which is now called <i class="calibre7">Holiday Summary</i><br class="calibre2"/> </li>
<li class="block_16">Navigate to your dashboard, using the left navigation as shown below<br class="calibre2"/><br class="calibre2"/><img alt="Image" class="calibre204" src="https://raw.githubusercontent.com/WebucatorTraining/skillable/main/55283/epub/images/image218.png"/><br class="calibre2"/> </li>
<li class="block_16">Drag, resize and position tiles on your dashboard until you are happy with the look (Delete the Holiday Requests.xlsx tile at the top-left of the dashboard by using the ellipsis (…))<br class="calibre2"/> </li>
</ol>
<table class="table_1">
<tbody class="calibre67"><tr class="calibre68">
<td class="td_8"><p class="block_49"><img alt="psTip32" class="calibre205" src="https://raw.githubusercontent.com/WebucatorTraining/skillable/main/55283/epub/images/image-68.png"/></p></td>
<td class="td_9"><p class="block_49"><i class="calibre206">Try not to click on a visual, as this will take you to the report that the visual came from, simply click and drag to position and use the </i><span class="text_9">drag handle</span><i class="calibre206"> </i><img alt="Image" class="calibre207" src="https://raw.githubusercontent.com/WebucatorTraining/skillable/main/55283/epub/images/image220.png"/><i class="calibre206"> at the bottom right of a visual to resize<br class="calibre208"/> </i></p></td>
</tr>
</tbody></table>
<p class="block_27"><img alt="Image" class="calibre209" src="https://raw.githubusercontent.com/WebucatorTraining/skillable/main/55283/epub/images/image221.png"/><br class="calibre2"/> </p>
<ol class="list_">
<li class="block_16" value="35">In the ribbon above the dashboard, click on<b class="calibre6"> Edit</b> then <b class="calibre6">Mobile view </b>(if you cannot see Edit in the ribbon, click on the <b class="calibre6">ellipsis (…) </b>)<br class="calibre2"/><br class="calibre2"/><img alt="Image" class="calibre210" src="https://raw.githubusercontent.com/WebucatorTraining/skillable/main/55283/epub/images/image-69.png"/><br class="calibre2"/> </li>
<li class="block_23">Take a moment to resize and position the tiles to optimise the dashboard for a mobile phone<br class="calibre2"/><br class="calibre2"/><img alt="Image" class="calibre211" src="https://raw.githubusercontent.com/WebucatorTraining/skillable/main/55283/epub/images/image-70.png"/><br class="calibre2"/> </li>
</ol>
<p class="block_" id="id_Toc10207240">Now you have a report with custom visuals and a <i class="calibre7">dashboard</i>. Remember that dashboards act as ways to aggregate visuals from multiple reports and pages. In the future if we build a new report from data based on the new holiday solution, we can use the same dashboard to bring the two reports together, old and new, for additional insights.</p>

# Exercise 2 – Setup Teams and create a list
<p class="block_">Next, we will utilise the Microsoft Team that you set up in Lab 6. We create a new channel for managing time off and add your Power BI report as a tab. We will then navigate to the SharePoint site that is linked to the Team and add a new SharePoint list to act as a data source for our Power App and trigger our flows. </p>
<ol class="list_">
<li class="block_15">Click on the <b class="calibre6">app launcher </b><img alt="Image" class="calibre15" src="https://raw.githubusercontent.com/WebucatorTraining/skillable/main/55283/epub/images/image.jpeg"/><b class="calibre6"> </b>and choose <b class="calibre6">Teams<br class="calibre2"/><br class="calibre2"/></b>If you see a welcome message inviting you to ‘Download the Teams desktop app and stay better connected’ ignore the <i class="calibre7">Get the Windows app</i> option and select <b class="calibre6">Use the web app instead<br class="calibre2"/> </b></li>
</ol>
<ol class="list_">
<li class="block_16" value="2">With the <i class="calibre7">Teams</i> tab selected on the left, click on the <b class="calibre6">ellipsis (…)</b> to the right of the Team you created in Lab 6 e.g. [Your Name] – IT Support<br class="calibre2"/><br class="calibre2"/><img alt="Image" class="calibre212" src="https://raw.githubusercontent.com/WebucatorTraining/skillable/main/55283/epub/images/image224.png"/><br class="calibre2"/> </li>
<li class="block_16">Choose <b class="calibre6">Add channel</b><br class="calibre2"/> </li>
<li class="block_16">Name the channel <b class="calibre6">Holidays</b> then click <b class="calibre6">Add</b><br class="calibre2"/> </li>
<li class="block_16">Make sure your new channel is selected, then in the tabs area click <b class="calibre6">Add a tab</b><br class="calibre2"/><br class="calibre2"/><img alt="Image" class="calibre213" src="https://raw.githubusercontent.com/WebucatorTraining/skillable/main/55283/epub/images/image-71.png"/><br class="calibre2"/> </li>
<li class="block_16">Select the <b class="calibre6">Power BI</b> tile (if you cannot see Power BI, use the search box to find it)<br class="calibre2"/> </li>
<li class="block_16">In <i class="calibre7">Tab name</i> enter <b class="calibre6">Holiday Report</b><br class="calibre2"/> </li>
<li class="block_16">Next, ensure <i class="calibre7">My Workspace</i> is expanded and then click on <b class="calibre6">Holiday Report</b><br class="calibre2"/><br class="calibre2"/><img alt="Image" class="calibre214" src="https://raw.githubusercontent.com/WebucatorTraining/skillable/main/55283/epub/images/image226.png"/></li>
<li class="block_16">Once ready click <b class="calibre6">Save</b>, and your report will be presented as a new tab<br class="calibre2"/><br class="calibre2"/><img alt="Image" class="calibre215" src="https://raw.githubusercontent.com/WebucatorTraining/skillable/main/55283/epub/images/image-72.png"/><br class="calibre2"/> </li>
<li class="block_16">Next, we will build a new SharePoint list to support our new holiday request solution, to get to the SharePoint site associated with this Team, Click on the <b class="calibre6">Files </b>tab then click on the <b class="calibre6">ellipsis (…)</b> in the ribbon and choose <b class="calibre6">Open in SharePoint</b><br class="calibre2"/><br class="calibre2"/><img alt="Image" class="calibre216" src="https://raw.githubusercontent.com/WebucatorTraining/skillable/main/55283/epub/images/image228.png"/><br class="calibre2"/> </li>
<li class="block_16">To navigate to your homepage, click on the <b class="calibre6">site icon</b><br class="calibre2"/><br class="calibre2"/><img alt="Image" class="calibre217" src="https://raw.githubusercontent.com/WebucatorTraining/skillable/main/55283/epub/images/image229.png"/><br class="calibre2"/> </li>
<li class="block_16">Next, on the homepage, click <b class="calibre6">+ New</b> then choose <b class="calibre6">List</b><br class="calibre2"/><br class="calibre2"/><img alt="Image" class="calibre218" src="https://raw.githubusercontent.com/WebucatorTraining/skillable/main/55283/epub/images/image-73.png"/><br class="calibre2"/> </li>
<li class="block_16">In the new pane on the right-side of the screen, enter the <i class="calibre7">Name</i> ‘Holiday Requests’ then click <b class="calibre6">Create</b><br class="calibre2"/> </li>
<li class="block_16">To design our data source, we will need columns to structure our table, to create a new selection of columns, proceed to click on the <b class="calibre6">+</b> to the right site of the Title column<br class="calibre2"/><br class="calibre2"/><img alt="Image" class="calibre219" src="https://raw.githubusercontent.com/WebucatorTraining/skillable/main/55283/epub/images/image-74.png"/><br class="calibre2"/> </li>
<li class="block_23">Next, create the following columns by adding a name and clicking <b class="calibre6">Save</b>:</li>
</ol>

<tbody class="calibre67"><tr class="calibre68">

</tr>

<p class="block_"><br class="calibre2"/> </p>
<ol class="list_">
<li class="block_15" value="16">Use the <b class="calibre6">+ New</b> button in the ribbon to create a new holiday request (use the account names Steve Smith and Chris Casingena to complete the form), once you have completed the form click on <b class="calibre6">Save </b>at the bottom<br class="calibre2"/><br class="calibre2"/><img alt="Image" class="calibre220" src="https://raw.githubusercontent.com/WebucatorTraining/skillable/main/55283/epub/images/image232.png"/><br class="calibre2"/> </li>
<li class="block_26">Your list is now ready, leave it open for our next exercise</li>
</ol>
