# Exercise 3 – Building the mobile holiday app
<p class="block_">Because you have created a data source (our SharePoint list) Power Apps can auto-build a usable app using its wizard. Once ready, we will change a few of the settings before publishing.</p>
<ol class="list_">
<li class="block_15">In the <i class="calibre7">Holiday Requests</i> list, in the ribbon, click on <b class="calibre6">Integrate </b>(if this button is not present, click on the <b class="calibre6">Ellipsis (…) </b>button) then choose <b class="calibre6">Power Apps</b>,<span class="text_8"> </span>then <b class="calibre6">Create an app</b> <br class="calibre2"/><br class="calibre2"/><img alt="Graphical user interface, text, application  Description automatically generated" class="calibre221" src="https://raw.githubusercontent.com/WebucatorTraining/skillable/main/55283/epub/images/image-75.png"/><br class="calibre2"/> </li>
<li class="block_16">Name the app <b class="calibre6">Holiday Requests</b> then click <b class="calibre6">Create<br class="calibre2"/> </b></li>
<li class="block_16">If asked to choose your country/region, make a selection and then click <b class="calibre6">Get started</b><br class="calibre2"/> </li>
<li class="block_16">In the <b class="calibre6">Home</b> tab of the ribbon, click on the <b class="calibre6">Theme </b>button this may be located under more options <img alt="Caret Right" class="calibre222" src="https://raw.githubusercontent.com/WebucatorTraining/skillable/main/55283/epub/images/image-76.png"/><br class="calibre2"/><br class="calibre2"/><img alt="Graphical user interface, application, Teams  Description automatically generated" class="calibre223" src="https://raw.githubusercontent.com/WebucatorTraining/skillable/main/55283/epub/images/image-77.png"/><br class="calibre2"/> </li>
<li class="block_16">Select a theme for your app<br class="calibre2"/><br class="calibre2"/><img alt="Image" class="calibre224" src="https://raw.githubusercontent.com/WebucatorTraining/skillable/main/55283/epub/images/image237.png"/><br class="calibre2"/> </li>
<li class="block_16">In the ribbon click on <b class="calibre6">Settings</b><br class="calibre2"/><br class="calibre2"/><img alt="Image" class="calibre225" src="https://raw.githubusercontent.com/WebucatorTraining/skillable/main/55283/epub/images/image-78.png"/></li>
<li class="block_16">In your app settings, choose a logo background colour and an icon (you can browse to a picture on your computer if you prefer)<br class="calibre2"/><br class="calibre2"/><img alt="Graphical user interface, text, application  Description automatically generated" class="calibre226" src="https://raw.githubusercontent.com/WebucatorTraining/skillable/main/55283/epub/images/image-79.png"/><br class="calibre2"/> </li>
<li class="block_16">Feel free to add a description, for example: <i class="calibre7">Submit a request for annual leave. Requests will be sent to your declared manager. </i><br class="calibre2"/> </li>
<li class="block_16">In the left navigation click on <b class="calibre6">Save</b> and once ready, click on the <b class="calibre6">Save </b>button<br class="calibre2"/> </li>
<li class="block_16">Next, click on <b class="calibre6">Publish</b><br class="calibre2"/><br class="calibre2"/><img alt="Image" class="calibre227" src="https://raw.githubusercontent.com/WebucatorTraining/skillable/main/55283/epub/images/image240.png"/></li>
<li class="block_16">Choose <b class="calibre6">Publish this version</b> once more<b class="calibre6"><br class="calibre2"/><br class="calibre2"/></b><img alt="Image" class="calibre228" src="https://raw.githubusercontent.com/WebucatorTraining/skillable/main/55283/epub/images/image241.png"/><b class="calibre6"><br class="calibre2"/> </b></li>
<li class="block_16">Next, in the left navigation click<b class="calibre6"> Close <br class="calibre2"/> </b></li>
<li class="block_26">Close the <b class="calibre6">Power Apps</b> tab in your browser (you may need to click <b class="calibre6">Leave</b> in the dialogue box) and once you return to your Holiday Request list, refresh the web browser <b class="calibre6">F5</b><br class="calibre2"/> </li>
</ol>

# Exercise 4 – Creating the approval process
<p class="block_">Now that we have an app, we can request holidays from mobile devices and other locations in Microsoft 365. But when the requests are received, they are simply stored as new rows of data in the SharePoint list. To allow the line manager to approve a request, we will use Power Automate to send the manager an approval request. We will then send an update to your Microsoft Team chat with the outcome.</p>
<ol class="list_">
<li class="block_15">In your <i class="calibre7">Holiday Requests</i> list, from the ribbon, click on <b class="calibre6">Integrate</b> &gt; <b class="calibre6">Power Automate </b>then choose <b class="calibre6">Create a flow</b> (the Integrate option may be in the <b class="calibre6">ellipsis (…)</b> menu)<br class="calibre2"/><br class="calibre2"/><img alt="Graphical user interface, application  Description automatically generated" class="calibre229" src="https://raw.githubusercontent.com/WebucatorTraining/skillable/main/55283/epub/images/image-80.png"/><br class="calibre2"/> </li>
<li class="block_16">In the <i class="calibre7">Create a flow</i> menu, select the template named <b class="calibre6">Start approval when a new item is added</b> <br class="calibre2"/><br class="calibre2"/><img alt="Image" class="calibre230" src="https://raw.githubusercontent.com/WebucatorTraining/skillable/main/55283/epub/images/image243.png"/><br class="calibre2"/> </li>
<li class="block_16">A new tab will open, if asked to choose your country/region, make a selection and then click <b class="calibre6">Get started</b><br class="calibre2"/> </li>
<li class="block_16">Scroll down on the template description and click on <b class="calibre6">Continue</b> to proceed (you may need to accept the sites cookies as it can cover up the Continue button)<br class="calibre2"/><br class="calibre2"/><img alt="Image" class="calibre231" src="https://raw.githubusercontent.com/WebucatorTraining/skillable/main/55283/epub/images/image-81.png"/><br class="calibre2"/> </li>
<li class="block_16">In the banner at the top of the page is the <i class="calibre7">Flow name </i>field, click here and rename the flow to <b class="calibre6">Holiday Request Approval</b> <br class="calibre2"/><br class="calibre2"/><img alt="Image" class="calibre232" src="https://raw.githubusercontent.com/WebucatorTraining/skillable/main/55283/epub/images/image-82.png"/><br class="calibre2"/> </li>
<li class="block_16">On the template, each action has an <b class="calibre6">ellipsis (…)</b> at the top right, use this ellipsis to access the <b class="calibre6">Delete </b>option and delete the following actions from the workflow:<br class="calibre2"/><img alt="Image" class="calibre233" src="https://raw.githubusercontent.com/WebucatorTraining/skillable/main/55283/epub/images/image-83.png"/><br class="calibre2"/> </li>
<li class="block_16">The result should match the diagram below:<br class="calibre2"/><br class="calibre2"/><img alt="Image" class="calibre234" src="https://raw.githubusercontent.com/WebucatorTraining/skillable/main/55283/epub/images/image247.png"/><br class="calibre2"/> </li>
<li class="block_16">Next, we need to pair our approval request with our approving line manager column in our holiday list, scroll up in the diagram to the <i class="calibre7">Start an approval</i> action and click into the <b class="calibre6">Assigned To</b> field<br class="calibre2"/> </li>
<li class="block_16">Click on the <b class="calibre6">Advanced mode</b> <img alt="Image" class="calibre235" src="https://raw.githubusercontent.com/WebucatorTraining/skillable/main/55283/epub/images/image248.png"/> button<br class="calibre2"/><br class="calibre2"/><img alt="Image" class="calibre236" src="https://raw.githubusercontent.com/WebucatorTraining/skillable/main/55283/epub/images/image249.png"/><br class="calibre2"/> </li>
<li class="block_16">Choose the property <b class="calibre6">Line Manager Email</b><br class="calibre2"/> </li>
<li class="block_16">In the green <b class="calibre6">If yes</b> branch below the condition action, click <b class="calibre6">Add an action</b><br class="calibre2"/><br class="calibre2"/><img alt="Image" class="calibre237" src="https://raw.githubusercontent.com/WebucatorTraining/skillable/main/55283/epub/images/image250.png"/><br class="calibre2"/> </li>
<li class="block_16">Search for ‘Team post’<br class="calibre2"/> </li>
<li class="block_16">In the resultant actions select <b class="calibre6">Post a message in a chat or channel</b><br class="calibre2"/><br class="calibre2"/><img alt="Text  Description automatically generated" class="calibre238" src="https://raw.githubusercontent.com/WebucatorTraining/skillable/main/55283/epub/images/image-84.png"/><br class="calibre2"/> </li>
<li class="block_16">Complete the actions configuration using the dynamic content pane (note that <i class="calibre7">Responder Ap… </i>is <i class="calibre7">Responder Approver Name</i>)<br class="calibre2"/><br class="calibre2"/><img alt="Graphical user interface, text, application, email  Description automatically generated" class="calibre239" src="https://raw.githubusercontent.com/WebucatorTraining/skillable/main/55283/epub/images/image-85.png"/><br class="calibre2"/> </li>
<li class="block_16">Click on the <b class="calibre6">ellipsis (…)</b> at the top right of the <i class="calibre7">Post a message as the Flow bot to a user</i> action and choose <b class="calibre6">Copy to my clipboard</b><br class="calibre2"/> </li>
<li class="block_16">In the <b class="calibre6">If no</b> branch of the condition click on <b class="calibre6">Add an action</b><br class="calibre2"/><br class="calibre2"/><img alt="Image" class="calibre240" src="https://raw.githubusercontent.com/WebucatorTraining/skillable/main/55283/epub/images/image253.png"/><br class="calibre2"/> </li>
<li class="block_16">Below the search bar, click on the <b class="calibre6">My clipboard</b> task<br class="calibre2"/><br class="calibre2"/><img alt="Image" class="calibre241" src="https://raw.githubusercontent.com/WebucatorTraining/skillable/main/55283/epub/images/image-86.png"/><br class="calibre2"/> </li>
<li class="block_16">Select the action you copied titled <b class="calibre6">Post a message in a chat or channel</b><br class="calibre2"/> </li>
<li class="block_16">Click on the new action to expand its configuration<br class="calibre2"/> </li>
<li class="block_16">Change the two references from <i class="calibre7">Approved</i> to <b class="calibre6">Rejected</b> so that the action resembles the configuration shown below<br class="calibre2"/><br class="calibre2"/><img alt="Graphical user interface, text, application, email  Description automatically generated" class="calibre242" src="https://raw.githubusercontent.com/WebucatorTraining/skillable/main/55283/epub/images/image-87.png"/><br class="calibre2"/> </li>
<li class="block_16">At the top of the page, click on <b class="calibre6">Save</b>, once saved review the flow, it will start when a new item is created in the list and then send an approval to the requesters line manager, if approved or rejected you are notified in Teams<br class="calibre2"/> </li>
<li class="block_16">Close the web browser tab for Power Automate (clicking <b class="calibre6">Leave </b>to confirm) and return to your browser tab with SharePoint<br class="calibre2"/> </li>
<li class="block_16">Next either select the browser tab with <b class="calibre6">Teams</b> already open or use the <b class="calibre6">app launcher </b><img alt="Image" class="calibre15" src="https://raw.githubusercontent.com/WebucatorTraining/skillable/main/55283/epub/images/image.jpeg"/><b class="calibre6"> </b>and navigate to <b class="calibre6">Teams</b> if you have closed this tab<br class="calibre2"/> </li>
<li class="block_26">In our last exercise we will test the solution by adding it to Teams as a tab then submit and approve a request</li>
</ol>

# Exercise 5 – Testing the solution
<p class="block_">Your workflow will now notify a member of staff if their request has been approved in the Teams chat. We will now test the new solution. To do this, we will add the app to our channel in Teams.</p>
<ol class="list_">
<li class="block_15">In the <i class="calibre7">Holiday</i> channel click on <b class="calibre6">Add a tab</b><br class="calibre2"/><br class="calibre2"/><img alt="Image" class="calibre243" src="https://raw.githubusercontent.com/WebucatorTraining/skillable/main/55283/epub/images/image256.png"/><br class="calibre2"/> </li>
</ol>
<ol class="list_">
<li class="block_16" value="2">Search for <b class="calibre6">Power Apps </b>and then select <b class="calibre6">Power Apps</b><br class="calibre2"/><br class="calibre2"/><img alt="Image" class="calibre244" src="https://raw.githubusercontent.com/WebucatorTraining/skillable/main/55283/epub/images/image257.png"/></li>
<li class="block_16">Choose <b class="calibre6">Add</b><br class="calibre2"/> </li>
<li class="block_16">Select your <b class="calibre6">Holiday Requests</b> app<br class="calibre2"/><br class="calibre2"/><img alt="Image" class="calibre245" src="https://raw.githubusercontent.com/WebucatorTraining/skillable/main/55283/epub/images/image258.png"/></li>
<li class="block_16">Next click <b class="calibre6">Save</b><br class="calibre2"/> </li>
</ol>
<ol class="list_">
<li class="block_16" value="6">Test the app by clicking <b class="calibre6">+</b> within the app to make a new holiday request<br class="calibre2"/> </li>
<li class="block_16">Fill out the form, ensuring that you put <b class="calibre6">your name</b> into the <i class="calibre7">Line Manager </i>field so that you can test the approval of a request, use Caroline Lee as your cover staff, once ready click on the <b class="calibre6">Tick</b> which will start your workflow (if you are having issues adding names to the people picker fields, click on the <b class="calibre6">Go to website</b> button and try in the new tab)<br class="calibre2"/><br class="calibre2"/><img alt="Image" class="calibre246" src="https://raw.githubusercontent.com/WebucatorTraining/skillable/main/55283/epub/images/image-88.png"/></li>
<li class="block_16">Click on the <b class="calibre6">app launcher </b><img alt="Image" class="calibre15" src="https://raw.githubusercontent.com/WebucatorTraining/skillable/main/55283/epub/images/image.jpeg"/><b class="calibre6"> </b>and choose <b class="calibre6">Outlook</b>, which should open a new tab, do not close the tab with Teams, we will return to it shortly<br class="calibre2"/> </li>
<li class="block_16">In your mailbox, select the approval email then choose <b class="calibre6">Approve</b>, optionally add comments and then choose <b class="calibre6">Submit</b> (if this has not appeared yet, it might take around 10 minutes at the longest, this is because the approvals service is being fired up for the first time)<br class="calibre2"/><b class="calibre6"><br class="calibre2"/></b><img alt="Image" class="calibre247" src="https://raw.githubusercontent.com/WebucatorTraining/skillable/main/55283/epub/images/image260.png"/><b class="calibre6"><br class="calibre2"/> </b></li>
<li class="block_23">Once you have submitted the approval for the holiday, return to the browser tab with <i class="calibre7">Teams</i> open, then click on the <b class="calibre6">Chat</b> button in the left navigation bar, you should see a card from Flow bot saying the request was approved<br class="calibre2"/><br class="calibre2"/><img alt="Image" class="calibre248" src="https://raw.githubusercontent.com/WebucatorTraining/skillable/main/55283/epub/images/image261.png"/><br class="calibre2"/> </li>
</ol>
<p class="block_">Although there is a lot of room for improvement, both functionally and aesthetically, this is a great proof of concept, leveraging the functionality of all three solutions and containing the experience within Teams which is the hub of the business.</p>

# Exercise 6 – Optional: Building a Microsoft Form
<p class="block_">If you have 5 minutes left for this exercise, it is worth trying out Microsoft Forms. Forms does not require the same level of instruction as the more complex Power Automate, Power Apps and Power BI solutions, therefore you can access it yourself and try building a quick survey. To begin, click on the <b class="calibre6">App launcher</b> and choose <b class="calibre6">All apps</b> then click on <b class="calibre6">Forms</b>.</p>
<p class="block_">Next, dismiss the welcome dialog then click on <b class="calibre6">New Form</b> to create a new survey. Think of a theme and title for your survey, for example, a customer satisfaction survey. Add suitable questions to the survey. Try the <b class="calibre6">Preview</b> button to check the appearance of your survey on a desktop or mobile view. Additionally, click on the <b class="calibre6">ellipsis (…)</b> at the top right of the page and take a look at the form <b class="calibre6">Settings</b> to discover ways to control the survey. Click on the <b class="calibre6">Share</b> button to review ways to share your survey.</p>
<p class="block_"><img alt="Image" class="calibre249" src="https://raw.githubusercontent.com/WebucatorTraining/skillable/main/55283/epub/images/image262.png"/></p>
<p class="block_22" id="calibre_pb_15"> </p>
